[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer/libFuzzer harness exercising Apache Commons Compress’s TAR support [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered a high-severity security finding: a Remote Code Execution [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m issue. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen parsing a specially crafted TAR archive entry, the library invokes Java [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization paths that allow unrestricted class or object instantiation based [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon external data. This was flagged as a `FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh: Remote Code [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExecution` by the fuzzer.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Issue manifestation  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – During `CompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`, the fuzzer feeds a malformed TAR[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive to Apache Commons Compress’s TAR reader.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – The code path enters `TarFile`, which constructs `TarArchiveEntry` instances by[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing header blocks.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – In `TarArchiveEntry.parseTarHeaderUnwrapped` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `parseTarHeader` and the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructor[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the implementation uses `ObjectInputStream.readObject` to populate [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfields. This leads to unguarded deserialization of attacker-controlled data.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – Reported as “Remote Code Execution.”  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – Root cause classification: unrestricted class/object creation via Java [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization of external data.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The stack trace pinpoints `Zer.readObject` → `ObjectInputStream.readObject` → [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveEntry.updateName`, indicating that entry names or metadata are [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialized without validation.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The fuzzer’s security API [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m explicitly flags the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlack of deserialization safeguards as exploitable.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The crash reproducer is generated as a Java test harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Crash_*.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirming that the vulnerability can be triggered in isolation by feeding the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrafted input to the TAR parsing routines.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Relevant code areas for investigation  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar.TarArchiveEntry`: in particular the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate methods `updateName` and `[0m[1;35mparseTarHeader[0m[1;39m([0m[39mUnwrapped[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – The use of `java.io.ObjectInputStream` within the TAR entry parsing logic.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – The constructors of `TarArchiveEntry` and `TarFile` where header data is read [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand deserialized.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – Any utility methods around deserialization or stream handling in [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.utils.IOUtils` that might influence object creation.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo analysis of potential fixes or speculative causes is included; this report [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfocuses solely on describing the observed security issue and pointing to the code [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocations most relevant for a complete review.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing run against the `CompressTarFuzzer` input triggered a [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh: Remote Code Execution` in the [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveEntry.updateName` method, where untrusted Base64‐encoded data was [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialized via `ObjectInputStream`. An attempted patch replaced the entire [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`updateName` implementation with a simple `return name;` to disable [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeserialization. However, the patch introduced mismatched braces and removed more [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode than intended, leading to widespread “class, interface, or enum expected” [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation errors in `TarArchiveEntry.java`.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer invoked `TarArchiveEntry.parseTarHeader` on malformed TAR data.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Within `[0m[1;35mupdateName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString name, String userName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, if `name` started with `[0m[32m"rO0"[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `userName` matched a sentinel, the code Base64‐decoded `name` and deserialized [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit via `ObjectInputStream`.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Jazzer flagged this as a high‐severity remote code execution vector, since [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary classes on the classpath could be instantiated.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines around [0m[1;36m1547[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m1568[0m[39m, the entire `if` block and deserialization logic were [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoved and replaced with:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ```[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Disable deserialization of entry names to prevent remote code execution[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return name;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ```[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The patch removed both the guard conditions and the deserialization branch, but [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdid not preserve or correctly re–insert matching closing braces for the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`updateName` method or its surrounding context.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch result  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The compiler reported ~[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m errors of the form “class, interface, or enum [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpected” and “<identifier> expected” throughout `TarArchiveEntry.java`.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- These errors indicate that the patch malformed the class structure [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextra or [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmissing braces[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, causing the entire remainder of the file to be parsed incorrectly.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for further investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `updateName` method signature and its surrounding braces in [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarArchiveEntry.java` to restore syntactic correctness.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The full `TarArchiveEntry` class around the original lines [0m[1;36m1547[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m1575[0m[39m to [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand the intended structure before and after the patch.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Any related methods that depend on `updateName` or on custom deserialization [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic in the TAR parsing flow.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The interplay between `parseTarHeader`, `TarArchiveEntry` constructors, and other[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutility methods that consume entry names.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
